---
layout: lexeme
lexeme: Mallasjuoma

###  Mallasjuoma₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Mallasjuoma* (malt drink)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  10
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  ORG
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
